                Canadian Pacific Railway buys Kansas City Southern to create 1st Canada-to-Mexico rail network
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">

             <h3 class="c-list__item__title">
              <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag-more-story-and-mosaic" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 20 06:59:00 EDT 2021" data-published-date=" Fri Mar 19 14:34:28 EDT 2021" id="article_status_PM Trudeau's pandemic promises: What was kept, what was broken?">

              <a class="c-list__item__link" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/politics/pm-trudeau-s-pandemic-promises-what-was-kept-what-was-broken-1.5354246" title="PM Trudeau's pandemic promises: What was kept, what was broken?">
               PM Trudeau's pandemic promises: What was kept, what was broken?
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              The federal government's made a lot of promises, including a flurry in the first six months of the pandemic. While some continue to make headlines, many others have hardly been spoken of since. CTVNews.ca examines what's become of those early pledges.
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/politics/pm-trudeau-s-pandemic-promises-what-was-kept-what-was-broken-1.5354246" title="PM Trudeau's pandemic promises: What was kept, what was broken?">

             <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag c-list__tag-lead-story" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 20 13:48:00 EDT 2021" data-published-date=" Thu Mar 18 21:53:12 EDT 2021" id="article_status_'Fight racism in all forms': How you can help Asian communities right now">
             </span>
             <h3 class="c-list__item__title">
              <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag-more-story-and-mosaic" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 20 13:48:00 EDT 2021" data-published-date=" Thu Mar 18 21:53:12 EDT 2021" id="article_status_'Fight racism in all forms': How you can help Asian communities right now">
              </span>
              <a class="c-list__item__link" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/canada/fight-racism-in-all-forms-how-you-can-help-asian-communities-right-now-1.5353493" title="'Fight racism in all forms': How you can help Asian communities right now">
               'Fight racism in all forms': How you can help Asian communities right now
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              The increased anti-Asian racism and violence during the COVID-19 pandemic, including the Atlanta mass shooting that targeted Asian spa workers, has caused global outrage and demands for more protections for Asian communities.
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/canada/fight-racism-in-all-forms-how-you-can-help-asian-communities-right-now-1.5353493" title="'Fight racism in all forms': How you can help Asian communities right now">

              </a>
             </h3>

              <a class="c-list__item__link" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/politics/don-martin-the-canada-u-s-partnership-roadmap-ignores-many-potholes-ahead-1.5321672" title="Don Martin: The Canada-U.S. 'partnership roadmap' ignores many potholes ahead">
               Don Martin: The Canada-U.S. 'partnership roadmap' ignores many potholes ahead
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              After four years of holding our collective breath following every prime ministerial meeting with the mercurial former U.S. president, Tuesday’s summit afforded a welcome sigh of relief at the happy harmony of it all, Don Martin writes in his exclusive column for CTVNews.ca.
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/politics/don-martin-the-canada-u-s-partnership-roadmap-ignores-many-potholes-ahead-1.5321672" title="Don Martin: The Canada-U.S. 'partnership roadmap' ignores many potholes ahead">

              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">

               What to expect when you're expecting… a signal from space
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              If aliens are sending us signals, are we set up to detect them? Dan Riskin speaks with planetary scientists, radio astronomers, and computer scientists who explain how the search for ET has ramped up in the last few decades. But if they're successful, is there a way to predict what alien creatures might look like?
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/what-to-expect-when-you-re-expecting-a-signal-from-space-1.5351231" title="What to expect when you're expecting… a signal from space">

             <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag c-list__tag-lead-story" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 13 09:00:00 EST 2021" data-published-date=" Wed Mar 10 16:03:58 EST 2021" id="article_status_How a powerful organization protects doctors from medical error claims">

             <h3 class="c-list__item__title">
              <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag-more-story-and-mosaic" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 13 09:00:00 EST 2021" data-published-date=" Wed Mar 10 16:03:58 EST 2021" id="article_status_How a powerful organization protects doctors from medical error claims">
              </span>
              <a class="c-list__item__link" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/how-a-powerful-organization-protects-doctors-from-medical-error-claims-1.5341894" title="How a powerful organization protects doctors from medical error claims">
               How a powerful organization protects doctors from medical error claims
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              Approximately 35,000 Canadians die every year as a result of medical errors in hospitals and long-term care facilities. Some families take the doctor to court, but physicians win the majority of cases. They are backed by a strong organization, called the Canadian Medical Protective Association, or CMPA.
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/how-a-powerful-organization-protects-doctors-from-medical-error-claims-1.5341894" title="How a powerful organization protects doctors from medical error claims">
              <div class="c-list__image">
               <picture>
                <source data-srcset="https://www.ctvnews.ca/polopoly_fs/1.5343050.1615477709!/httpImage/image.jpg_gen/derivatives/landscape_620/image.jpg" media="(min-width: 400px)" srcset="https://www.ctvnews.ca/polopoly_fs/1.5343050.1615477709!/httpImage/image.jpg_gen/derivatives/landscape_135/image.jpg"/>

                <img alt="The Canadian Medical Protective Association provides doctors with legal support in court to fight malpractice suits." data-src="https://www.ctvnews.ca/polopoly_fs/1.5343050.1615477709!/httpImage/image.jpg_gen/derivatives/landscape_800/image.jpg" src="https://www.ctvnews.ca/polopoly_fs/1.5343050.1615477709!/httpImage/image.jpg_gen/derivatives/landscape_135/image.jpg"/>

               Mark Carney's journey from money man to climate change crusader
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              The former governor of both the Bank of Canada and Bank of England, is on a crusade. Mark Carney wants everyone to think differently about what's valuable in our natural world and he’s shared how that might be achievable with W5.
             </p>

             </span>
             <h3 class="c-list__item__title">
              <span class="c-list__item__status c-list__tag-more-story-and-mosaic" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 06 09:02:00 EST 2021" data-published-date=" Wed Mar 03 15:04:23 EST 2021" id="article_status_One year later: Why Canada's COVID-19 crisis is being called a 'senicide'">
              </span>
              <a class="c-list__item__link" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/one-year-later-why-canada-s-covid-19-crisis-is-being-called-a-senicide-1.5332262" title="One year later: Why Canada's COVID-19 crisis is being called a 'senicide'">
               One year later: Why Canada's COVID-19 crisis is being called a 'senicide'
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              March 8th 2021 marks one year since Canada's first death from COVID-19, a senior in a long-term care facility in British Columbia. Since then 55 per cent of all deaths have been long-term care residents. It has been described as a senicide: the killing of the elderly or their abandonment to death.
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/one-year-later-why-canada-s-covid-19-crisis-is-being-called-a-senicide-1.5332262" title="One year later: Why Canada's COVID-19 crisis is being called a 'senicide'">
             </a>
             <p class="c-list__item__date" data-last-modified="Sat Mar 06 09:02:00 EST 2021" data-published-date="Wed Mar 03 15:04:23 EST 2021">
             </p>
            </div>
           </article>

              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="c-list__item__description" tabindex="0">
              W5 investigates Canada's controversial practice of flying live horses around the world to be slaughtered for fresh, raw, horsemeat. The campaign to stop the live horse export has ramped up with the celebrity endorsement of Canadian singer Jann Arden, who calls it the 'sinister side of agriculture.'
             </p>
             <a class="c-list__item__image" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/w5/a-glimpse-inside-canada-s-sinister-horse-meat-industry-1.5324002" title="A glimpse inside Canada's 'sinister' horse meat industry">

  <script type="text/javascript">
   const config = {
        rootMargin: "25px",
        threshold: 1.0
    };

    let preloadImage = (element) => {
        if(element.dataset && element.dataset.src) {
            element.src = element.dataset.src;
        }
        if(element.dataset && element.dataset.srcset) {
            element.srcset = element.dataset.srcset
        }
    }
    let onIntersection = (entries) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
            if (entry.intersectionRatio > 0) {
                observer.unobserve(entry.target);
                preloadImage(entry.target);
            }
        });
    }

    const images = document.querySelectorAll('source, img');
    if (!('IntersectionObserver' in window)) {
        Array.from(images).forEach(image => preloadImage(image));
    }
    else {
        observer = new IntersectionObserver(onIntersection, config);
        images.forEach(image => {
            observer.observe(image);
        });
    }
  </script>
